 ) sena or sainya abhiyaanon kii tasviren chunavi abhiyaan main istemaal na kii jaaen
 The Election Commission has given this advice to all political parties
 chunaav ayog ne sabhi raajnneetik dalon se kaha he ki ve apane chunaav abhiyaan main sainikon or sainya abhiyaanon kii tasveeron kaa istemaal karne se bachein
 The Election Commission on Saturday, citing consultations issued in 2013, asked the heads of all political parties to ensure strict adherence to their party representatives and candidates
 ayog ne ek raajnneetik dal ke poster main vaayu sena wing commander abhinandan kii tasviir ke kathith istemaal par sangyaan lete hue raajnneetik dalon ko aisa karne se bachane kaa paraamarsh diya he
 It is noteworthy that the Commission issued this consultation in December 2013 on the complaint of the Ministry of Defense
 isamen mantralay ne vibhinn raajnneetik dalon ke ummidavaaron dwaara chunaav abhiyaan main sanyakarmiyon kii tasviir kaa istemaal karne par chunaav ayog kaa dhyaan aakarshith karte hue ise rokane ke liye upyukt nirdesh jari karne kaa anurodh kiya tha
 The Commission, in its consultation, stated that the security forces are the neutral guard of the security of the country's borders and political system
 aise main raajnneetik dalon or unke netaaon ko apane chunavi abhiyaan main sainya balon ke sandarbh kaa kisi bhi rup main sahaara lete samay atyadhik saavdhaanee baratane kii jarurat he
 In view of this, political parties and their candidates should not use military forces personnel and photographs of military operations etc
 in the election campaign
 ayog ne raajnneetik dalon ke pramukhon se apane netaaon evam ummidavaaron ko sainikon or sainya abhiyaanon kii tasviir kaa istemaal karne se bachane kaa nirdesh jari karne ko kaha he
 (from input language) america kii united airline ke vimaan main savaar ek mahila ne bhedbhaav kii shikaayat kii he
 The woman alleges that her previously booked seat was changed to two "muslim religious leaders" because they did not want to sit next to a woman
 mairi campos california se huston jane vaale vimaan main savaar thim
 He explained that the airline changed his seat because "he is a woman and two men did not want to sit close to a woman
" " sibisi local kii report ke mutabik mairi ko nayaa boarding paas dete vakt isaki vajah yah bataai gai ki do yatri apni "dharmik manyataon" ke chalate kisi mahila ke paas nahin baith sakate hai or na hi ve kisi mahila se baat kar sakate hai
 Mary was told that the men wearing long orange shirts are Pakistani religious leaders
 mairi ke mutabik mahila karmchaariyon dwaara un do purushon ko bhojan bhi nahin parosane diya gaya
 He said, "half of the population here cannot be discriminated against based on the beliefs of another country
 " report ne mairi ke hawaale se kaha he, "meraa maananaa he ki ham aisi samskruti main rahete hai jahaan mahilaon ko purushon ke baraabar mana jaataa he
 "it states that Mary was stunned by this incident but had no other option but to take a new seat
 tippaniyan In a letter to United Airline, Mary stated, "no one who believes in such recognition should travel on a commercial plane
 " airline ne ek vaktavy jari kiya he jisamen kaha gaya he, "seat badale jane kaa shrimati compos ko bura laga, is baat kaa hamen khed he
 United expect their employees to be of the highest level of professionalism and zero tolerance against discrimination
